  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8911215e-9433-4eb9-8518-641175e058af'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer1856435495900837144"><b><i>Chain of Gold</i>, a Shadowhunters novel, is the first novel in a brand-new trilogy where evil hides in plain sight and love cuts deeper than any blade. .</b><br/><br/>Cordelia Carstairs is a Shadowhunter, a warrior trained since childhood to battle demons. When her father is accused of a terrible crime, she and her brother travel to London in hopes of preventing the family’s ruin. Cordelia</span>
  <span id="freeText1856435495900837144" style="display:none"><b><i>Chain of Gold</i>, a Shadowhunters novel, is the first novel in a brand-new trilogy where evil hides in plain sight and love cuts deeper than any blade. .</b><br /><br />Cordelia Carstairs is a Shadowhunter, a warrior trained since childhood to battle demons. When her father is accused of a terrible crime, she and her brother travel to London in hopes of preventing the family’s ruin. Cordelia’s mother wants to marry her off, but Cordelia is determined to be a hero rather than a bride. Soon Cordelia encounters childhood friends James and Lucie Herondale and is drawn into their world of glittering ballrooms, secret assignations, and supernatural salons, where vampires and warlocks mingle with mermaids and magicians. All the while, she must hide her secret love for James, who is sworn to marry someone else.<br /><br />But Cordelia’s new life is blown apart when a shocking series of demon attacks devastate London. These monsters are nothing like those Shadowhunters have fought before—these demons walk in daylight, strike down the unwary with incurable poison, and seem impossible to kill. London is immediately quarantined. Trapped in the city, Cordelia and her friends discover that their own connection to a dark legacy has gifted them with incredible powers—and forced a brutal choice that will reveal the true cruel price of being a hero.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1856435495900837144" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

<div id="review_698061167" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="gio" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23204207-gio"><img alt="gio" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597613414p2/23204207.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/698061167?book_show_action=true">Aug 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="gio" class="user" itemprop="url" name="gio" href="/user/show/23204207-gio">gio</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23204207-gio?shelf=2020-releases">2020-releases</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer698061167" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10320818987402220716">2.5 stars<br/><br/>Oof this book. It’s objectively a hot mess. Objectively pretty bad, as it is:<br/><br/>- 50% drama<br/>- 20% misunderstandings<br/>- 20% escamotage from a beautiful episode <br/>- 10% actual things happening <br/><br/>Like, my rational side (which is 90% of my own personality) would give this one 2 stars and the series a goodbye 👋 <br/>BUT. It was fun. DRAMATIC FUN BUT FUN. I was honestly the popcorn.gif the whole time or most of it. I rolled my eyes a couple of times, but lord, I was entertained. <br/><br/>If you want a break down of </span>
  <span id="freeText10320818987402220716" style="display:none">2.5 stars<br /><br />Oof this book. It’s objectively a hot mess. Objectively pretty bad, as it is:<br /><br />- 50% drama<br />- 20% misunderstandings<br />- 20% escamotage from a beautiful episode <br />- 10% actual things happening <br /><br />Like, my rational side (which is 90% of my own personality) would give this one 2 stars and the series a goodbye 👋 <br />BUT. It was fun. DRAMATIC FUN BUT FUN. I was honestly the popcorn.gif the whole time or most of it. I rolled my eyes a couple of times, but lord, I was entertained. <br /><br />If you want a break down of what’s objectively not good in this book:<br /><br />- the plot is thin, or even nonexistent tbh. This book is 590 pages and I could probably sum up the events in 3 sentences. <br />- the drama has reached unbelievable highs. This book makes Clockwork Prince look tame (if it wasn’t set in the early 20th century this would totally be PWP with angst on Ao3).<br />- Clare has decided that everyone needed to be a main character. Only, you can’t make 15 characters the main character, because none of them ends up having a clear and distinct voice or personality beyond a few thinly described characteristics. And this is exactly what happens here: Cordelia, James and Lucie should be the main characters but to be quite honest they weren’t the most interesting ones and they weren’t more well developed than say, Anna or Matthew and we know very little about the latter. <br /><br />But this was still fun. You could still enjoy it if you were looking for:<br /><br />- a lot of hot people being stupidly in love with the wrong person or believing themselves to be in love with the wrong person (or right person really, depends who you ask).<br />- a LOVE POLYGON (don’t ask me how many sides it has tbh).<br />- Anna, light of the whole book who should 100% be the main character of this book damn. <br /><br />Honestly I’m ashamed of myself giving this 3 stars, but I’m trash and I fully intend to be trash for the rest of the series, because I want to see how much more fucked up it can get.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10320818987402220716" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8829575056177268653">Note December 18, 2018: With much regret I requested that GR freezes the comments for this review. I am tired of constantly getting alerts and having to delete harassment. I really don't know why people can't get it into their thick heads that this is my review. They can disagree with it, but they don't have to come on here and attack me. God, just grow up already. <br/><br/>Disclaimer: Fanbots and trolls will be blocked. I don't care if you think I'm mean to Cassandra Clare. I really doubt she's read thi</span>
  <span id="freeText8829575056177268653" style="display:none">Note December 18, 2018: With much regret I requested that GR freezes the comments for this review. I am tired of constantly getting alerts and having to delete harassment. I really don't know why people can't get it into their thick heads that this is my review. They can disagree with it, but they don't have to come on here and attack me. God, just grow up already. <br /><br />Disclaimer: Fanbots and trolls will be blocked. I don't care if you think I'm mean to Cassandra Clare. I really doubt she's read this review and I doubt she's hurt by it. I really don't care if you think these books are great and that having a grand total of eighteen plus books in a series is a good idea. If you want to whine about it write your own damn review. <br /><br />Let me tell you a little story, boys and girls. It's how to over milk a series.<br /><br />Pre Step One: Start a ridiculous popular fan fic that you later use for the basis on your work. Never mind the fact you might occasionally borrow quotes and passages from other sources. If you get enough reviews you'll get noticed and eventually.....hello, publishing contract.<br /><br />Step One: Write a fairly decent YA series. It doesn't have to be great, but decent enough to have interest and a catchy theme that you can use over and over again. It also helps if you get a blurb from Stephenie Meyer.<br /><br />Step Two: Come up with a spin off (note, spin off should be fairly decent and better than the original).<br /><br />Step Three: Restart first series even though it had a decent ending so you can add in future conflicts. Add a bunch of annoying characters and unnecessary plot to claim there's room for more story.<br /><br />Step Four: Sell movie rights after a substantial amount of time so you don't look like a sell out and build a substantial fan base.<br /><br />Step Five: Graphic novel adaptions. Note, once spinoff is successful rinse and repeat step five.<br /><br />Step Six: After your first series starts sagging and your second series is about to wrap up announce a new series in addition to a lot of info books about your world.<br /><br />Step Seven: Edit your own info books and gets your b.f.f.s to write the essays so they portray you in the best light. Also, state you and your hubby are going to write a guide to your own universe as well. Because hey, info books worked for Stephenie Meyer and JK Rowling has mentioned a Harry Potter encyclopedia throughout the years as well. So that must be the cool thing to do.<br /><br />Step Eight: Get your b.f.f.s to help you write a spinoff with your best character-spread this out over time so you can keep getting those royalties.<br /><br />Step Nine: After second series wraps up and the hype for your movie starts announce you'll be writing at least two more series (it also helps if final book in said series has a family tree which will make fanoholics want to know what happens with these characters and write fan fic that might be better than your own work).<br /><br />Step Ten: Relish in the green. You're a true success now. Also work on licensing out games, toys, etc. Heck, maybe you can get your own theme park/production company if you're successful enough.<br /><br />Amendment Post City of Heavenly Fire:<br /><br />1) Pimp your new series with brand new characters in your last book. So that it's almost a prequel to that series. And furthermore, feature your other spinoff so fans and people who want to know what's actually going on other than feeling stupid the entire book, will have to read the eight other books prior to this epic finale.</span>

<div id="review_3168306480" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3168306480" />
    <a title="Kai" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/41788524-kai"><img alt="Kai" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1573562141p2/41788524.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3168306480?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kai" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kai" href="/user/show/41788524-kai">Kai</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41788524-kai?shelf=queer">queer</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41788524-kai?shelf=owned">owned</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3168306480" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3069139033116331654">me: I'm never gonna read a Shadowhunter book again<br/>me: NEVER<br/>me: Mortal Instruments is a MESS<br/>me: never<br/>me: the Infernal Devices finale s u c k s<br/>me: nope<br/>me: the Bane chronicles are so bad I cried<br/>me: n e v e r<br/>me:<br/>me: I'm so gonna read this book<br/><br/>Fellow reader, after giving up Shadowhunters for good...I fell victim to them once more. And surprisingly, I think I enjoyed myself?<br/><br/>Let's state the obvious, I really liked CC's writing style in CoG, her period Shadowhunter novels just have that romantic atmosphe</span>
  <span id="freeText3069139033116331654" style="display:none">me: I'm never gonna read a Shadowhunter book again<br />me: NEVER<br />me: Mortal Instruments is a MESS<br />me: never<br />me: the Infernal Devices finale s u c k s<br />me: nope<br />me: the Bane chronicles are so bad I cried<br />me: n e v e r<br />me:<br />me: I'm so gonna read this book<br /><br />Fellow reader, after giving up Shadowhunters for good...I fell victim to them once more. And surprisingly, I think I enjoyed myself?<br /><br />Let's state the obvious, I really liked CC's writing style in CoG, her period Shadowhunter novels just have that romantic atmosphere that comes with a more antiquated and elegant style of writing. I also found the characters much (much) less irritating than Clary, Jace, Will and most of that whole messy bunch. Apart from Magnus that is. I think he is overused and badly written and I just don't enjoy having to read about him. But even James and Matthew seemed less annoying than their predecessors. Their edges are softened and they're not totally unbearable when it comes to self-centredness and the urge to feel pity for yourself 24/7 while looking dramatically gorgeous.<br /><br />But, while we're at it, I do find it boring that every single character is beautiful. If everyone is beautiful, the world gets boring. SJM makes the same mistake and it results in characters becoming soulless and interchangeable. Also, eyes like "pale gold tea"? Oh <i>please</i>. I imagine CC sits in her writing room and just pulls random adjectives out of a glass jar. Well, what eye colour will our character have today? Muddy sapphire it is.<br /><br />I believe that the cast of characters was way too big. CC might know them inside out but whoah it was a lot to take in and eventually I stopped trying to keep everyone apart. They blurred into each other, and I also found myself not caring who lived or died cause I didn't know who they were to begin with. I did like that multitude of queer characters, mostly because there can never be too many queer characters. I've seen people criticise her representation of them and saying that she merely included them to make her book more diverse. Personally, I could not find anything wrong with how the queer characters were written, although I am concerned about Anna Lightwood - who cannot be older than 20 - and the many immortals that have had an affair with her. That feels a bit iffy.<br /><br />The story was engaging. It was slightly predictable, especially considering who would end up with whom. But I am intrigued to find out what happens in the sequels, and it feels like CoG was merely a setup for books two and three. The plot wasn't overly dramatic, so I expect the stakes will be much higher in the future. I genuinely enjoyed reading it, and even though it was almost 600 pages, it was a quick and entertaining read. I guess the many alternating POVs make it more engaging. What I don't enjoy is CC turning the last 100 pages into a soppy epilogue. She did this with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18335634.Clockwork_Princess__The_Infernal_Devices___3_" title="Clockwork Princess (The Infernal Devices, #3) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Princess</a> and it resulted in me wanting to throw the book out of the window. And she did it once more with CoG. The final showdown happens around the 500 page mark, but we get about 90+ more pages of plot and nothing really happens? I find that very irritating.<br /><br />Kudos though to CC including a more diverse set of poets and writers in this book. I remember her doing this ever since <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/256683.City_of_Bones__The_Mortal_Instruments___1_" title="City of Bones (The Mortal Instruments, #1) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Bones</a>: every chapter is introduced with a quote from Dickens, Yeats, the bible. But this time around, it wasn't just dead white men, I spotted a selection of female writers and a beautiful traditional Persian tale that was also woven into the main plot. Thumbs up for that.<br /><br />So yes, even though nothing can get me to read TDA or her novella collections, I really want to know what happens next in this series.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.instagram.com/kaispellmeier/" rel="nofollow noopener">Find more of my books on Instagram</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="3069139033116331654" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2030617844" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2030617844" />
    <a title="✨ A ✨ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/65321843-a"><img alt="✨ A ✨ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604503440p2/65321843.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2030617844?book_show_action=true">Nov 14, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✨ A ✨ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✨ A ✨ " href="/user/show/65321843-a">✨ A ✨ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781406392" href="/book/show/52128971-chain-of-gold">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=cross-post">cross-post</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=four-and-half-stars">four-and-half-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=2020-release">2020-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=gifted">gifted</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=faves-ya-scifi-and-fantasy">faves-ya-scifi-and-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=read-in-2020">read-in-2020</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2030617844" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12420453544224653894"><b>Me:</b> ahahaha I'm so over Cassie Clare. She's really just milking this series. Gosh when will she stop with the recycled tropes?!<br/><b>Also me:</b> I would die a thousand deaths for Will Herondale and his babies <br/><br/><i>[ a list of the short stories that feature the crew from Chain of Gold can be found at the end of this review ⤵️]</i><br/><br/>The Shadowhunters of the London Institute have had 10 years of peace. The younger generation have been raised surrounded by love and with little exposure to the hardships their parents fa</span>
  <span id="freeText12420453544224653894" style="display:none"><b>Me:</b> ahahaha I'm so over Cassie Clare. She's really just milking this series. Gosh when will she stop with the recycled tropes?!<br /><b>Also me:</b> I would die a thousand deaths for Will Herondale and his babies <br /><br /><i>[ a list of the short stories that feature the crew from Chain of Gold can be found at the end of this review ⤵️]</i><br /><br />The Shadowhunters of the London Institute have had 10 years of peace. The younger generation have been raised surrounded by love and with little exposure to the hardships their parents faced in their youth. For some odd reason demons have been avoiding London. But that changes when the Carstairs and Blackthorn families move to the city. <br /><br />A series of demon attacks leave several Shadowhunters poisoned and London goes on lock down. Nobody in, nobody out. And no help from the rest of the Clave. <br /><br />Cordelia Carstairs along with her soon to be parabatai Lucy Herondale her brother James and his friends find themselves not entangled in the search for answers and a cure. <br /><br />Friendships, secrets, betrayal and love - this book is everything we adore about the Shadowhunter Chronicles <br /><br /><i>
  <b>“The point of stories is not that they are objectively true, but that the soul of the story is truer than reality. Those who mock fiction do so because they fear the truth.”</b>
</i><br /><br />TID was one of my favourite series ever. So when Cassie announced she'd be writing about the next generation of Herondales/Carstairs/Lightwoods/Fairchilds I, like everyone one else in this fandom, freaked out! <br /><br />Yes it took years of patience, but it's finally here and it did not dissapoint.<br /><br />To me the plot felt splendidly thought out. This is a generation raised by loving parents with hardly any need for them to fight demons. But still, none of them are perfect, they all have they own problems. The reason I thought this was so, is because as we all know, YA authors are fond of killing off the protagonists parents. Happy and whole families just aren't a normal feature in YA. So it was really interesting to see how Cassie would tackle this.<br /><br />I quickly came to adore the characters but that is probably helped by the fact that I am familiar with them due to all the short stories and snippets Cassie has releases over the years. <br /><br />In true CC fashion, we had a group of friends who love each other fiercely and who, despite knowing they shouldn't, take it upon themselves to get things done while the adults and the Clave argue and bicker. <br /><br />Cordelia was an awesome MC. She is fierce and sweet and loyal, but also a bit lonely. I loved how welcoming the Merry Theives were to her. <br /><br />I absolutely <i>loved</i> getting to know more about Cortana. Like wow, I thought that sword was amazing before but now I'm just in awe. Gotta get me one of those 😂. <br /><br /><blockquote>“I never quite thought of friendship like that—as something that makes you more than you are.”</blockquote><br /><br />The Merry Thieves were precious. I loved their dynamic, their banter and how much they care for each other. I also liked James's place as leader. <br /><br /><blockquote>“Each of you follows his own star—but you are the thread that binds all four together. You are the one who sees what everyone needs, if anyone requires extra care from their friends, or even to be left alone. Some groups of friends drift apart, but you would never let that happen.”</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>“Do not let those who cannot see the truth tell you who you are. You are the flame that cannot be put out. You are the star that cannot be lost. You are who you have always been, and that is enough and more than enough. Anyone who looks at you and sees darkness is blind.”</blockquote><br /><br /><br />So yes, this book is jam packed with new characters I love. But there were also ones I hated. <i>*cough*Grace, Charles, Tatiana*cough*</i><br /><br />The only reason I didn't give a full five stars is because I thought there was one trope the CC is recycling once again that everyone is tired of and was really unnecessary. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[yet again another love triangle *sigh* <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />The ending was fantastic. It has me so desperate for the next book and I sincerely hope we get it soon!<br /><br /><i>‹ Thank you to the publishers for sending me a copy in exchange for an honest review ›</i><br />_____<br /><br /><b>• WHAT TO READ OR RE-READ BEFORE CHAIN OF GOLD •</b><br /><br />When they said you can read this without reading of the previous Shadowhunter books, <b>THEY LIED</b>. A lot of people were confused and couldn't keep track of all the characters and families. At least read <i>The Infernal Devices</i> before jumping into this. If you haven't read <i>Chain of Gold</i> yet and wondering which short stories feature our crew from <i>CoG</i> that you might want to reread, I've made a list: <br /><br /><b>The Bane Chronicles:</b> <br /><u>4. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17334074.The_Midnight_Heir__The_Bane_Chronicles___4_" title="The Midnight Heir (The Bane Chronicles, #4) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">The Midnight Heir</a></u> - [very important!!] about James Herondale, set just before COG <br /><br /><b>Tales from the shadowhunter academy:</b> <br /><u>3. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23380999.The_Whitechapel_Fiend__Tales_from_the_Shadowhunter_Academy___3_" title="The Whitechapel Fiend (Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy, #3) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">The Whitechapel Fiend</a></u> - about Tessa and Will and the kids are still babies. Not very relevant to COG but still interesting to see domestic will/tessa<br /><u>4. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24365190.Nothing_but_Shadows__Tales_from_Shadowhunter_Academy___4_" title="Nothing but Shadows (Tales from Shadowhunter Academy, #4) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Nothing but Shadows</a></u> - [important] James at the academy <br /><br /><b>Ghost of the Shadow market:</b> <br /><u>2. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/37955374.Cast_Long_Shadows__Ghosts_of_the_Shadow_Market___2_" title="Cast Long Shadows (Ghosts of the Shadow Market, #2) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Cast Long Shadows</a></u> - [important] about Matthew Fairchild<br /><u>3. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/37955375.Every_Exquisite_Thing__Ghosts_of_the_Shadow_Market___3_" title="Every Exquisite Thing (Ghosts of the Shadow Market, #3) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Every Exquisite Thing</a></u> - about Anna Lightwood <br /><br />______<br /><b>My reviews for:</b><br /><br /><i>The Infernal Devices Series</i><br />Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3182520676" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Angel</a><br />Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3182522112" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Prince</a><br />Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3182523415" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Princess</a><br /><br /><i>[Sorry no reviews for TMI, I read it too long ago and don't plan to re-read]</i><br /><br /><i>The Dark Artifices Series</i><br />Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2324804598" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Midnight</a><br />Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1930668614" rel="nofollow noopener">Lord of Shadows</a><br />Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1930668787" rel="nofollow noopener">Queen of Air and Darkness</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12420453544224653894" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1636381081" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1636381081" />
    <a title="Beth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44125660-beth"><img alt="Beth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600268807p2/44125660.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1636381081?book_show_action=true">May 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth" href="/user/show/44125660-beth">Beth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781406358094" href="/book/show/43175835-chain-of-gold">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=faves">faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=march-reads">march-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=lgbtqa">lgbtqa</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=swoony-swoony">swoony-swoony</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=the-tears-are-real">the-tears-are-real</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=2020-reads">2020-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=characters-i-loved">characters-i-loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=book-series">book-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1636381081" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10639483105328631200"><b>By the Angel 5 Stars!</b><br/><br/><i>”We do not get to choose when in our lives we feel pain,” said Matthew "It comes when it comes, and we try to remember, even though we cannot imagine a day when it will release its hold on us, that all pain fades. All misery passes. Humanity is drawn to light, not darkness.”</i><br/><br/>I want to make this very, very clear that I am very much a Cassie Clare fan, The Infernal Devices is my favourite series and holds a very special place in my heart, so you can imagine my pure delight when</span>
  <span id="freeText10639483105328631200" style="display:none"><b>By the Angel 5 Stars!</b><br /><br /><i>”We do not get to choose when in our lives we feel pain,” said Matthew "It comes when it comes, and we try to remember, even though we cannot imagine a day when it will release its hold on us, that all pain fades. All misery passes. Humanity is drawn to light, not darkness.”</i><br /><br />I want to make this very, very clear that I am very much a Cassie Clare fan, The Infernal Devices is my favourite series and holds a very special place in my heart, so you can imagine my pure delight when I found out that Chain of Gold was coming out I was so excited to see my favourite characters once more and get to explore their lives as parents. What I <u>didn’t</u> expect was to fall in love with a whole new group of Shadowhunters (well I did, just not so quickly). <br /><br />Before I begin I want to give a MASSIVE shout out to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2184360779?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Katie</a> for Buddy Reading this with me. Many melt downs, listening to my theories and then telling me some of yours (just saying we nailed it in some parts). I thought I was going to enjoy it either away, but reading it with you made the experience so much more special so thank you!<br /><br />If you’re going to read this I strongly suggest you read The Infernal Devices at a minimum but there are lots of little nods to other novellas throughout and in particular a story with a certain character is brought to light in a particular novella.<br /><br />The story starts off a little slow HOWEVER, I think it was needed. There are <u> a lot</u> of new characters, and it was interesting to see and learn the dynamic of them all. We are back in London and there has been something strange going on… there is no sightings of demons, however more and more attacks keep cropping up and some of them happen at lets say questionable times and the result of this makes the Shadowhunter have to come together and sort through a plan. <br /><br />When you compare it to the other books in this world it is its own book, there are some similarities in the sense of strong bonds, something is going on and the younger generation are going to investigate, but some of the usual cliches we see such as forbidden romance, a love triangle are not there and I think it made it it’s own. Just to point out that the love triangle in both TID and TDA are one of my favourites and the forbidden love trope is always <b>*Chef Kiss*</b>. This had the absolute <i>perfect</i> balance of having TID references in, there wasn’t too much where it became over bearing and it was sometimes so subtle other than the mentions of worms and demons… still gets me overtime, but the story <u>is</u> itself.<br /><br />Before going into the character portion of this review I want to point out that I have seen some negativity towards having so many LGBTQ+ Characters and I am completely baffled. I just want to point out a few things, it is always important to have representation in a book and Cassandra Clare always brings that. This is a fantasy book that has half Angels, Demons, Warlocks, Ghosts and many more but you can’t see why there are so many LGBTQ+ people? Finally just because in the 1900s people weren’t always outspoken about their sexuality and/or gender doesn’t mean it didn’t happen. I personally loved seeing so much diversity within the characters!<br /><br /><b>Added Bonus of Will and Tessas’ Wedding</b><br /><br />Going into this, I knew hands down that I would cry. I just knew it, it just made me feel so happy and overjoyed BUT it also made me feel ridiculously sad just thinking about Jem. I think what made it so special was Charlottes words, the added touches with the Cane (I AM DESTROYED OKAY). It was even better than anything I could of asked for. I hope we get more little snippets of them in their twenties just living their life, because it makes me so ridiculously happy it’s crazy!<br /><br /><u>Characters</u><br /><br />We have a new set of Shadowhunters for me to cry over and love with all of my heart and here are just some of my thoughts, just to warn you I will be gushing away, in a quick round up I genuinely really liked 90% of the characters, despised a few handful and intrigued about others but I have a feeling that they will come into it a lot more as the story continues.<br /><br /><i>”That’s everyone’s dream, isn’t it, really? Instead of many who give you a little piece of themselves, one who gives you everything”</i><br /><br /><b>Cordelia</b> right now is probably my favourite of the new characters. We’ve seen a lot of female characters by Cassie, but I think Cordelia brings something new and exciting. She doesn’t think she’s the best, she works and trains so hard, painfully loyal to her friends and family. I low key kind of love her relationship with Alastair in the sense that she sees herself as the annoying younger sister and just wants to be thee for him which was SO sweet and she really puts herself on the line for other people. <b>You know!</b><br /><br />We have super sweet <i>Lucie</i>. For me personally Lucie has a super interesting arc that I don’t want to go too much into because of spoilers but one chapter in particular was <u>so</u> well executed I was sat there screaming at my book like OH MY GOD! It was just amazing. Lucie and Cordelias relationship is lovely and you can see that they both well and truly care about one another, I am invested in this friendship hands down!<br /><br /><b>Anna</b> is SUCH an interesting character. After reading about her in the novella in Ghosts of The Shadow Market I was very excited to see her in this. I love her attitude, and you can see how much she cares. Her continuous love interests and her reactions had me dying it was just so funny. This is one more character I can’t wait to read more about! To quote Anna… <i>”They didn’t… and neither did you.”</i><br /><br />Keeping it 100, I am not a fan of <i>Grace</i>. I just, from the very start I did not trust her what so ever. She was just too “perfect” and sickly sweet and I just couldn’t work her out, as the story progressed I just disliked her even more, saying this I am very very interested to find out more about her.<br /><br /><u>The Merry Thieves</u><br /><br /><i>”But we suffer for love because love is worth it.”</i><br /><br />Where to begin with <b>James</b>? To start off you can tell he is Wills’ son, he has that easy charm but then he is like Tessa in the sense that he is quite a calming presence. I loved seeing him with the shadows and how relationships progressed. He stepped up to a “leader” role and you can see how much he cares.<br /><br /><i>Matthew</i> is probably the most complex out of the shadow hunters, and it is very useful to of read his backstory. I really really feel for him in Chain of Gold. He has an issue when it comes to alcohol and sometimes like to play the fool. You can see his unyielding protection and love when it comes to James and there are some truly heartfelt moments. Out of all of the shadow hunters this time around Matthew is my favourite male (sorry, but Cordelia is my Queen right now).<br /><br /><i>”We don’t always love people who deserve it”</i><br /><br />I’m finding it slightly hard to talk a lot about <b>Thomas</b> and <i>Christopher/Kit</i> so I think it’s easier to merge them together for this book. I can see a story arc playing out for Thomas very clearly in my mind, and I am here for it, but after things panned out I’m wondering HOW&gt;! As for Christopher I think out of all of the characters he’s the least I know about, hopefully we will get to see more!<br /><br />Just to point out the next Characters aren’t part of The Merry Thieves and I know that particularly in Chain of Gold Matthew and Thomas take more of a centre stage compared to Grace and Anna but I didn’t want to break them up!<br /><br />Out of all of the character I feel the most conflicted towards <b>Alastair</b>, you can see SO much potential with him, and he is such an interesting character. He’s quite mysterious and we do learn little bits about him (not all good either) and I was well and truly on my way to full on rooting for him, I mean I still am but I’m kind of angry with him as well!<br /><br />I’m saying it now I LOVE <i>Jesse</i>, he’s such an interesting character and his relationship with Lucie was one of my favourites. The interactions they have I was just oohing and ahhing, but he is so selfless and my heart literally broke at one point for him. I think that as the story progresses I am intrigued to see what’s going to happen with him. <br /><br /><i>You let me be something I had never been before, even when I was living. A Shadowhunter.</i><br />We got to see <b>Papa and Mama Herondale AKA Will and Tessa</b> and it was so lovely to see them being parents! I think what was so sweet was how much there loved showed even after all of those years together. You see their protective sides come out when it came to their children, nieces and nephews. You still got to see Wills silly and fun loving side and Tessa with her fondness. You still get so many lovely quotes from these two and see them in a different light. They’re still the same but just with the view of being parents and slightly more mature!<br /><br /><i>”A better Shadowhunter and a better man,” said Will. “All the best of me, I learned from Jem and your Mother...”</i><br /><br />Finally last but not least we get <i>Jem</i>, it’s interesting to see him in his Silent Brother role, but with him still knowing who he truly is. I adored his interactions with the younger generation and the older ones and he really is that figure that many people look to for some form of guidance and knowledge. Even though I expected it and I KNOW what happens with his story Arc up until a certain point it still breaks my little heart. <br /><br />What I <b>liked?</b><br />- Lets state a few obvious ones in a bulk here: Back into the Shadowhunter world I go, <b>Will Herondale, my number one book love</b>, seeing so many people from TID, my heart was so happy, SO many references to TID I was overjoyed!<br />- So much love and friendship, honestly I don’t care what anyone says, the friendships across these books are always so well done<br />- Seeing little snippets of Jem, Will and Tessa had me weeping, by 90 pages in I’d cried twice.<br />- Some of the more “action” scenes had me completely gripped, they were done so well and I could just see it all playing out, it was so intense and had me gripped!<br />- <i>Cortana</i> I found it super interesting this time around, we all know about Cortana but I’m pretty sure it did something I haven’t seen it do before and I was like oooooh gurl<br />- It had me questioning <u>a lot</u>, I thought I had some things figured out and then something would happen and it would completely flip my opinion.<br />- Horses… and while we’re on it even though they’re not linked what so ever. Ghosts.<br />- The Warlocks that are Malcolm and Hypatia, it was interesting to see a reference in this knowing what we do I was like OOOOOH<br />- SO MUCH SIBLING LOVE!<br />- The amount of times I must of said “What is going on”<br />- Sending of dresses and Sonas reaction, I just knew who had sent them it was great<br />- A certain Herondale Star popping up… consistency is key!<br />- Magbus turning up <u>six hours</u> early and his response being “bloody hell” it was hilarious!<br />- All of the tension… ooooft<br />- OSCAR, who’s a good boy!<br />- A erm, certain locket and what is inside it…<br />- Gideon and Gabriel, oh I missed my favourite brothers!<br />- Hair colours…<br /><br />I’m just going to say, that where it left off I am feeling very very anxious for what’s to come but I’m so excited, one whole year! Guess the countdown will begin, but I am very very excited!<br /><br />What I <b>didn’t like?</b><br /><br />My <u>only</u> complaint is I wish we’d see more of Anna, Christopher and Thomas. I think from this first book we only got a slight glimpse into who they are, however that means that we will hopefully get to see a lot more of them as the series continues!<br /><br /><i>“But at least we can always pick up a book and read it anew. Stories offer a thousand fresh starts.”</i><br /><br />Final thoughts…<br /><br />My heart is so full with happiness, I can’t begin to explain how much these books and stories mean to me. I think because of my love for The Infernal Devices I was scared to see how this would pan out, but it was <u>so</u> enjoyable and I literally cannot wait for book 2 to be released! <br /><br />---------<br />09.03.2020<br /><br />By The Angel!<br /><br />That was hands down one of my most anticipated reads of the year and it did not let me down what so ever!<br /><br />What an amazing introduction to the start of the New Years.<br /><br />Currently sobbing my head out at Will and Tessas wedding but I knew I was going to!<br /><br />Full review to come and just to warn you it will more than likely be a long one cause your girl is OBSESSED<br />————<br /><br />03.03.2020<br /><br />Happy release day for Chain of Gold! Hope you all have the best time reading it!<br /><br />Secretly jealous because Amazon ruined it and I haven’t got my copy even though I preordered it when it first came out...<br /><br />Let’s hope I get my Waterstones delivery tomorrow :)<br /><br />————-<br /><br />02.03.2020<br /><br />TOMORROW THIS WILL ARRIVE... I get to see my love again!<br /><br />I also booked off Wednesday cause I’m that person who needs personal time with their books...<br /><br />————<br />15.01.2020<br /><br />It is the year 2020, in less than two months Chain of Gold will be here, I will have at least four copies and two book boxes of this, and if you dare be terrible and not give these character ALL of the love I will Riot (Zoe will join me as well)<br /><br />—————<br />13.12.18<br />LOOK AT THAT COVER I AM IN LOVE!<br />————<br />28.07.18 <br />So I’m reading TID (Clockwork Prince) and it’s just dawned on me.<br />Page 300<br />“We who are immortal, we are chained to this life by a <b>chain of gold</b>, and we dare not sever it for fear of what lies beyond the drop” said Magnus<br /><br />Coincidence? I think not!<br />—————<br />When you need a book more than life itself, because your one true love is finally coming back to you... I. need. this. <b>now.</b><br /><br />WILL HERONDALE, sooooooooooooon!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10639483105328631200" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2074475892" />
    <a title="Samantha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10067920-samantha"><img alt="Samantha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590018789p2/10067920.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2074475892?book_show_action=true">Mar 24, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Samantha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Samantha" href="/user/show/10067920-samantha">Samantha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2074475892" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2791233594690068646">3.75 stars - This book is exactly what I wanted right now. I’ve only previously read The Infernal Devices, but I enjoyed this for the same reason I enjoyed that series: it’s follows a bunch of beautiful people in love and there’s barely any plot. The fantasy world is a fun but fairly unimportant backdrop to the angst and romance of the characters. And I couldn’t be happier! I go into these books with those expectations and I am not disappointed. These are the book equivalent of a CW tv show (and</span>
  <span id="freeText2791233594690068646" style="display:none">3.75 stars - This book is exactly what I wanted right now. I’ve only previously read The Infernal Devices, but I enjoyed this for the same reason I enjoyed that series: it’s follows a bunch of beautiful people in love and there’s barely any plot. The fantasy world is a fun but fairly unimportant backdrop to the angst and romance of the characters. And I couldn’t be happier! I go into these books with those expectations and I am not disappointed. These are the book equivalent of a CW tv show (and I say that as a fan of CW shows for the same reason — pretty people who all love each other!) <br /><br />While technically these series can be read separately because Clare does a good job of recapping important bits from other series and the Shadowhunter world in general, I can’t imagine reading it without TID. There’s too many characters from TID and too many references that make the book more fun if you understand them. <br /><br />There are so many characters in here that at one point I had to draw a chart to outline how everyone was related and who liked who, but I caught on quickly after that. This was a fun romp with likable characters and plenty of angst and romance tropes to enjoy. But it did drag on a bit towards the end and would have been better as a shorter book. <br /><br />I will be doing a full review and discussion in my channel :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="2791233594690068646" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1123355430" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1123355430" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1123355430?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=2020-reads">2020-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=historical-fiction">historical-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1123355430" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10573313522087956633"><b>I was desperate to read this book.</b><br/><br/>I’ve been part of the world of the Shadowhunters for more than ten years, The Infernal Devices being my favorite saga. I clung to the memories of the London Institute, of holy water and blood, of crushed hearts and clockwork angels and faded <i>parabatai</i> runes through happy times and difficult times, ever since I finished <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18335634.Clockwork_Princess__The_Infernal_Devices___3_' title='Clockwork Princess (The Infernal Devices, #3) by Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>Clockwork Princess</a>. When my hands touched <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17699853.Chain_of_Gold__The_Last_Hours___1_' title='Chain of Gold (The Last Hours, #1) by Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>Chain of Gold</a>, when I breathed in its pages and sank into the familiar lives of the Nephilim, it felt l</span>
  <span id="freeText10573313522087956633" style="display:none"><b>I was desperate to read this book.</b><br><br>I’ve been part of the world of the Shadowhunters for more than ten years, The Infernal Devices being my favorite saga. I clung to the memories of the London Institute, of holy water and blood, of crushed hearts and clockwork angels and faded <i>parabatai</i> runes through happy times and difficult times, ever since I finished <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18335634.Clockwork_Princess__The_Infernal_Devices___3_" title="Clockwork Princess (The Infernal Devices, #3) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Princess</a>. When my hands touched <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17699853.Chain_of_Gold__The_Last_Hours___1_" title="Chain of Gold (The Last Hours, #1) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Chain of Gold</a>, when I breathed in its pages and sank into the familiar lives of the Nephilim, it felt like I returned home after a long, bittersweet journey. And yet… And yet a part of me, a guilty part of me wishes that The Last Hours trilogy would remain a distant hope, an expectation rather than a fact.<br><b>A part of me wishes it were never written.</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Whither thou goest, I will go, James. Even unto the tedious suburb of Highgate.”</i>
</blockquote><br>The Shadowhunters have grown soft. Demonic activity is scarce, leaving room for frivolity and other mundane pleasures. But old debts must be paid, and a terrible storm is brewing, aiming to destroy the Nephilim once and for all. In the center of this new conspiracy, there is one of mixed heritage. Half angel, half demon, James Herondale and his friends shall fight, lie, bleed in order to uncover the mystery behind the irregular massacres and the poison that has infected the London Enclave, before it is too late.<br><blockquote>
  <i>“We don’t always love people who deserve it.”</i>
</blockquote><br>I can hear my younger self shouting expletives. <i>You were gifted with more time with Will</i>, she says. <i>With Edwardian Shadowhunters. With demon slaying and cosmic friendships and did I mention <b>Will and Tessa as parents</b>?</i> It is true, my soul rejoiced and clenched and drowned in <b>nostalgia and longing</b>. The tether that binds it with the world of the Nephilim remained firm, and I fell in love with the new generation (with James and Lucy and Cordelia and Matthew and Thomas and Christopher and Anna and Jesse), I loathed some evil spawns (Grace and Charles), I am confused about my feelings for others (yes Alastair, that’s you) and in general, <b>I was lost in a place where I always found myself</b>. And yet, there are reasons <b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17699853.Chain_of_Gold__The_Last_Hours___1_" title="Chain of Gold (The Last Hours, #1) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Chain of Gold</a> felt discordant</b>. Like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/150038.Cassandra_Clare" title="Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Cassandra Clare</a> was playing a song she has mastered but missed a couple of notes, and I can attribute it to two factors.<br><br><b>First</b>, the Shadowhunters Chronicles are no strangers to death. Many beloved characters have perished, leaving fresh wounds in their wake. However, I never wanted to experience such losses through the eyes of the teenagers I once rooted for so deeply. Will, Tessa, Sophie, Gideon, Cecily, Gabriel, Henry, Charlotte, they went through so much that it seems unfair to witness their lives unfold in a manner that will break them. I would prefer the ideal picture I built in my head about their happily ever afters free of revenge, pain and loss. <b>The price of watching them become parents is simply too steep</b>.<br><br><b>Second</b>, a famous ingredient of the Shadowhunter Chronicles is teenagers rebelling against the adults who refuse to listen. In the past, the Clave has been a de facto enemy, the corrupt or scared or stubbornly ignorant authority that forces our valiant heroes to sneak, steal and lie in order to save the world. Now, <b>the Clave consists of said heroes</b>. That’s why <b>all the secrets and unnecessary risks seem so mind-numbingly stupid</b>. It’s <b>
  <i>Will Herondale</i>
</b>. It’s <b>
  <i>Tessa Gray</i>
</b>. It’s <b>
  <i>Charlotte Branwell</i>
</b>. It’s <b>
  <i>Gabriel and Gideon Lightwood</i>
</b>. <b>Why, by the Angel, did Cassandra have to present lame excuses and misguided promises in order to keep the parents in the dark?</b> They would assist, they would dive into danger headlong <b>because they value and trust their children</b>. Instead their children lied to their faces, withheld vital information and that was a stab in the heart. <b>A betrayal to the heroes of The Infernal Devices</b>. <br><blockquote>
  <i>“Did you expect more fear? Then you do not know my father. You do not know my mother. You do not know my family, or me.”</i>
</blockquote><br>On a more cheerful note, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17699853.Chain_of_Gold__The_Last_Hours___1_" title="Chain of Gold (The Last Hours, #1) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Chain of Gold</a> was <b>equal parts painful, engaging and amusing</b>, as expected. The relationships <b>tangled</b> as ever. And the characters? They were shooting starts. <b>Vibrant</b>. Burning brightly and fiercely, with love being their greatest strength and most dangerous weakness.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1589024572i/29443431.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/cassiejp/" rel="nofollow noopener">Art by Cassandra Jean</a><br><br><b>The Merry Thieves are heart stealers.</b> The leader, the scientist, the libertine, the kind one, with the addition of the Beautiful Cordelia (slay Queen, slay) and none other than the aspiring author, ghost-whisperer Lucie, they are all my <b>cinnamon rolls</b> who <b>must.be.protected.at.all.costs</b>. As for the romances? You didn’t expect simple, did you? <b>Forbidden, hopeless, devastating, that’s <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/150038.Cassandra_Clare" title="Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Cassandra Clare</a>’s way, and the road ahead is paved with suffering and pain</b>. And even though I mentally prepared myself to deal with it, there are already cracks in my armor that will eventually leave me exposed to the tragedies which are bound to happen.<br><br><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17699853.Chain_of_Gold__The_Last_Hours___1_" title="Chain of Gold (The Last Hours, #1) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Chain of Gold</a> was the beginning of a powerful story of revenge, blood and love which will undoubtedly wreak unimaginable emotional havoc. <br>I am equal parts excited and terrified.</b><br><br>P.S. Did it ever occur to you that for people bound by the holiest of bonds, the <i>parabatai</i> never talk to each other about their romantic aspirations? I sincerely hope that history shall not be repeated, and a love triangle similar to The Infernal Devices will be avoided. Because once was quite enough.<br><br><b>P.P.S. WILLIAM OWEN HERONDALE IS STILL THE LOVE OF MY LIFE MY HUSBAND MY SUN AND STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1489261769ra/22200594.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="10573313522087956633" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2878222924" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2878222924" />
    <a title="Whitney Atkinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14457130-whitney-atkinson"><img alt="Whitney Atkinson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1550868411p2/14457130.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2878222924?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Whitney Atkinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Whitney Atkinson" href="/user/show/14457130-whitney-atkinson">Whitney Atkinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=read-in-2020">read-in-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=lgbtqiap">lgbtqiap</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=need-to-buy-asap">need-to-buy-asap</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2878222924" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14027890333524276185">If you're a Cassie Clare fan, ignore this review because you're gonna love the book. But if you're like me, with not enough brain cells to fathom rereading every Shadowhunter book and every little novella in between, you should probably read this book with the Shadowhunters wiki page pulled up in another tab. <br/><br/>I'll give this book its credit where it's due: I think Chain of Gold features my favorite cast of characters yet. Usually in Cassandra Clare worlds, I'll only be able to locate two or three</span>
  <span id="freeText14027890333524276185" style="display:none">If you're a Cassie Clare fan, ignore this review because you're gonna love the book. But if you're like me, with not enough brain cells to fathom rereading every Shadowhunter book and every little novella in between, you should probably read this book with the Shadowhunters wiki page pulled up in another tab. <br /><br />I'll give this book its credit where it's due: I think Chain of Gold features my favorite cast of characters yet. Usually in Cassandra Clare worlds, I'll only be able to locate two or three characters I care deeply for and I skip the chapters of the rest. In Chain of Gold, however, I loved every character. You get the perfect balance of being reunited with old characters (ahhem, jem step on my neck) whilst falling in love with new ones (matthew and anna, stomp on me). The writing is great, this book is transporting, all is well. <br /><br />But Cassie Clare books have ceased to be books that you can read with little effort. Because this book follows characters who have novellas about them already, you're expected to go into this with a lot of background knowledge. I had none. And I was baffled for nearly 300 pages before I finally stopped to Google everything. I hope the final copy has a family tree or a character guide to spare y'all the time. There are easily 10-15 moments in this book where the characters are like "hahaha remember when this happened??" in reference to the events of a previous novella, meanwhile I'm just chillin' with crickets in the background because I wasn't told there was an entire prequel to this new trilogy. I'm not sure if I'd go as far as to call it lazy storytelling to require so much extra reading on top of the 600 pages of development in this book, but it was definitely annoying that I felt I was witnessing the middle of a character arc rather than the beginning of it. <br /> <br />Even though I grew to love the characters (after I was finally able to distinguish who was who), not much happened in this book. If I were going to spoil you, there's probably only two or three major events to describe. Although this was one of my most anticipated releases of 2020, I found myself procrastinating picking it back up to read because it just isn't that exciting. I'm giving it a bit of credit because it's the first book in a series setting up the plot, but for a 600-page book, it was still a bit excruciating at times.<br /><br />Another disappointment was the romance. It felt like there was none except one or two scenes, even though the synopsis almost revolves around Cordelia's crush on James. (Side note: It's a stretch to consider Cordelia the main character of this book. It follows the entire cast of characters almost equally.) This book lacked the angst of Cassie's previous books, though likely because a majority of the build-up and action occurred in previous novellas. Also, the time period makes sexuality and lust a lot more taboo, so that might have played a factor in why there was so little action I craved. <br /><br />All I've said sounds super negative, but once I got into the groove of this book, I really did adore it. There's lots of nods to previous series with Will and Tessa and Magnus and Cortana and certain little Easter eggs that were so fun to find. Part of the reason this book wasn't 5 stars for me is entirely user error since I didn't read the prequel novellas, but I'm also just disappointed that Cassie Clare books from now on are going to be so difficult to read because they'll have required you to read her 20+ book series arc just to understand the basic premise and characters. So although this book took a sec to get through, I'm really looking forward to the sequel and I would like to thank not only God but Jesus that we've been spared too much of a cliffhanger.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14027890333524276185" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_580400581" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/580400581" />
    <a title="Jude" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4418048-jude"><img alt="Jude" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483571062p2/4418048.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/580400581?book_show_action=true">Apr 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jude" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jude" href="/user/show/4418048-jude">Jude</a>
      </span>

          marked it as to-read




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4418048-jude?shelf=00-ugh">00-ugh</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer580400581" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13475693584685907878"><a href='http://s1231.photobucket.com/user/JudeHnd/media/GIFS/tumblr_mdd3z9ctRH1r5jxm3_zpsdd90539f.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416187ra/821859.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mdd3z9ctRH1r5jxm3_zpsdd90539f.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Here We Go Again.</b><br/><br/>First, I want to make clear to everyone that I Looooove TMI and TID, Loved them. But there's already The Dark Artifices coming and now <i>this</i>? <br/><br/>The thing about lots of books in a series is that, for them to work well, the author has to built this whole excellent world that is just so well written and so thought of that you can't help but want continue to be in it - for example Harry Potter. The Nephilim world is amazing and I've loved learning more and more about it and I can't</span>
  <span id="freeText13475693584685907878" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1231.photobucket.com/user/JudeHnd/media/GIFS/tumblr_mdd3z9ctRH1r5jxm3_zpsdd90539f.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416187ra/821859.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mdd3z9ctRH1r5jxm3_zpsdd90539f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Here We Go Again.</b><br><br>First, I want to make clear to everyone that I Looooove TMI and TID, Loved them. But there's already The Dark Artifices coming and now <i>this</i>? <br><br>The thing about lots of books in a series is that, for them to work well, the author has to built this whole excellent world that is just so well written and so thought of that you can't help but want continue to be in it - for example Harry Potter. The Nephilim world is amazing and I've loved learning more and more about it and I can't seem to get enough of CC's books but.... no more.<br><br>Let's think about TMI and TID for a minute.... they are different periods of time and yada yada... but what are the similar things??? ....Oh Hell, I'll just say it: <b>Characters.</b> Now please don't hate me for this, but Will is Jace, Jem is Simon, Jessamine is/was Isabel just as Tessa was Clary. Of course there were differences, like how Clary was more... feisty? not sure if that's the word I want to use, but whatever. While Tessa has a more quiet strength in her. <i>Still</i>, they are <i>very</i> similar. <br><br>The same theory that applies to the story applies to the characters: Jace for example, was an Amazing character to read, he was refreshing, funny, charming, EVERYTHING. Which is why it did not bother me <u>at all</u> to see the same qualities in Will, but... but.... no more. <br><br>CC is an amazing writer, but I would just love to see something new from her. She seems to have so much potential and I really think she has the talent to create a whole other new world, with more new and refreshing characters, I would just really like to see her explore that side. <br><br>That being said... <i>maybe</i> I'll read her new Nephilim books. I did not continue reading the second part of TMI, but I did love the whole TID series... I just think that too much of something can really be a turnoff. Personal opinions people, I just felt like ranting. <br></span>

<div id="review_2649652895" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2649652895" />
    <a title="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17438949-melissa-dog-wolf-lover-martin"><img alt="Melissa ♥ Dog/Wolf Lover ♥ Martin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603831478p2/17438949.jpg" /></a>

<span id="freeTextContainer9568938672432943256"><b>The Infernal Devices nostalgia is real with this one!!</b><br/><br/>This is now my favorite Cassandra Clare book yet! I absolutely love and adore these characters so much! It brought back all the same emotions I had while reading The Infernal Devices and it made me so happy! I think the London institute is by far my favorite. <br/><br/>This book also had so much action and lots of demon fights, which is what I always look for with Cassandra Clare books! I loved every character so much! Anna Lightwood was definitely my </span>
  <span id="freeText9568938672432943256" style="display:none"><b>The Infernal Devices nostalgia is real with this one!!</b><br /><br />This is now my favorite Cassandra Clare book yet! I absolutely love and adore these characters so much! It brought back all the same emotions I had while reading The Infernal Devices and it made me so happy! I think the London institute is by far my favorite. <br /><br />This book also had so much action and lots of demon fights, which is what I always look for with Cassandra Clare books! I loved every character so much! Anna Lightwood was definitely my favorite, I cannot wait to read more about her!<br /><br />Overall, I enjoyed this book so much and I don’t have any issues! Cannot wait for the next book! <br /><br />Also did a video on my YouTube channel where I discussed my thoughts more while reading, you can watch it here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://youtu.be/N5M8uWyWNMU">https://youtu.be/N5M8uWyWNMU</a></span>

<div id="review_1579173924" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1579173924" />
    <a title="✨    jamieson   ✨" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7706640-jamieson"><img alt="✨    jamieson   ✨" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499961431p2/7706640.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1579173924?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✨    jamieson   ✨" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✨    jamieson   ✨" href="/user/show/7706640-jamieson">✨    jamieson   ✨</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781406392" href="/book/show/52128971-chain-of-gold">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=historical-fiction">historical-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=2020-reads">2020-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=owned-books">owned-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=series-to-complete">series-to-complete</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1579173924" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9569924454293518841">I'm undetermined on if I didn't like this as much as previous Cassandra Clare books because my reading tastes are just not the same anymore, or if it was because it was just genuinely not that well written? This felt so long and the plot really dragged in places, actually, I think the plot was really weak? No real interesting villains and not much tension to hold the book together. That said, I really am only here for the characters and for hot people in angsty love which I got a lot of. I liked</span>
  <span id="freeText9569924454293518841" style="display:none">I'm undetermined on if I didn't like this as much as previous Cassandra Clare books because my reading tastes are just not the same anymore, or if it was because it was just genuinely not that well written? This felt so long and the plot really dragged in places, actually, I think the plot was really weak? No real interesting villains and not much tension to hold the book together. That said, I really am only here for the characters and for hot people in angsty love which I got a lot of. I liked James, Cordelia, Anna and Matthew as characters and I liked Cordelia/James dynamic as well as Cordelia/Alistair's sibling relationship. I wasn't sure if I would continue this series but then /something/ happened at the end that forces me to highly consider it because I LOVE THE TROPE. <br /><br />Overall, I think perhaps I just love Lady Midnight (2016) so much all future Clare books will be a let-down. That said, I really was just looking for something enjoyable I didn't have to think about to read on a rainy day and this did work perfectly for that. </span>
  <a data-text-id="9569924454293518841" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
